Author: Jeremy Benoist <jeremy.benoist@gmail.com>
Date:   Thu Feb 3 14:48:18 2022 +0100

    Make ESLint & Prettier works together
    
    `indent` & `array-bracket-spacing` conflicts so it's better to remove it from ESlint and let Prettier handle these cases.

commit 6975610cccf87ce8f69389c74c8546de4123aabf
Author: Jeremy Benoist <jeremy.benoist@gmail.com>
Date:   Thu Feb 3 14:07:59 2022 +0100

    Fix tests with Serverless v3
    
    The new serverless class must have 3 options for its argument.
    
    ```
    // before
    serverless = new Serverless();
    
    // after
    serverless = new Serverless({ commands: ['print'], options: {}, serviceDir: null });
    ```
    
    Also:
    - remove useless `prettier-eslint-cli` which isn't compatible with ESLint 8 and also isn't necessary (we can use `prettier` directly)
    - move all `*.tests.js` file into the `tests/` folder (easier to find them)
    - require node 12

commit 6a3b99600f70dbf6b7aeaebf96714f246e7b4563
Merge: dc4be8a eed3382
Author: Jérémy Benoist <j0k3r@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Tue Aug 31 06:13:17 2021 +0200

    Merge pull request #944 from mostthingsweb/patch-1

commit eed33820c8cdc596187d9b606c44b9115d4263c1
Author: Chris Laplante <mostthingsweb@gmail.com>
Date:   Sun Aug 29 18:24:24 2021 -0400

    Fallback on using service provider runtime / 'nodejs'
    
    When using "sls deploy function --function=function-name",
    serverless-webpack would crash if the runtime was not set explicitly for
    the function. This patch makes behavior consistent with other accesses
    to the function runtime, falling back on the service provider's runtime
    (or 'nodejs') if the function doesn't declare a runtime.

    Skip container function with `uri` defined

Merge: 4c4b4f1 8096608
Author: Jérémy Benoist <j0k3r@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Wed May 5 20:08:09 2021 +0200

    Merge pull request #813 from serverless-heaven/fix/spawn-e2big-zip-error

commit 809660819a960dba053aa25d62146436a8339a6c
Author: Jeremy Benoist <jeremy.benoist@gmail.com>
Date:   Wed May 5 12:22:48 2021 +0200

    Fix call to `hasNativeZip`

commit b828e0f0b481e736195d448e7ec962804f4274d5
Author: Jeremy Benoist <jeremy.benoist@gmail.com>
Date:   Wed May 5 11:57:15 2021 +0200

    Fix the `spawn E2BIG` error when zipping
    
    When the native method to zip is used, we give it a list of all files to be included in the archive.
    Because of `node_modules`, that list can be very huge and then we hit a limit which broke the build with `spawn E2BIG` error.
    
    We list files because we might need to filter them if the `excludeRegex` option is used.
    So, the zip method is now forced to node in case of that option is defined.
    Otherwise, we are using the method available (which might be the native one in most case) and we don't give it a list of files to be zipped but a folder (we don't use `*` because it'll omit dot files).

    Display the zip method used
    
    Since 5.4.0 we are using `bestzip` which can improve performance by using native `zip` method if available instead of the node one.
    But we don't know which method is used during the build, so improving a small log to know that information.
    
    ```
    Serverless: Zip service (using native zip method): /project/.webpack/service [11882 ms]
    ```
    
    Also:
    - run `npm audit fix` to fix some vulnerabilities.
    - improve / cleanup return data from mocks

commit d17097ab4be6a4f453d86c2cb3c7ba401ad604e4
Author: Daniel Sellers <dsellers@instructure.com>
Date:   Fri Jan 4 17:40:51 2019 -0700

    <!--
    1. Do not remove any section of the template. If something is not applicable leave it empty but leave it in the PR
    2. Please follow the template, otherwise we'll have to ask you to update it and it will take longer until your PR is merged
    -->
    
    Closes #433
    
    <!--
    Briefly describe the feature if no issue exists for this PR. If possible only
    submit PRs for existing issues. If the PR is trivial (like doc changes or simple
    code fixes) it can be submitted without a related issue, but as soon as it adds
    or changes functionality, a related issue should be present.
    -->
    
    Fairly trivial, just used the ignore option in glob to exclude files matching the glob.
    
    1. Setup a serverless project with an index.test.js and an index.js that handle a route
    2. Start it up and see that you get a warning about duplicate files matching for index
    3. Now pull in this PR
    4. add the following to your serverless.yml file in the custom > webpack section
    `excludeFiles: **/*.test.js`
    5. restart serverless
    6. see that the warnings are now gone!

    - [x] Fix linting errors
    - [x] Make sure code coverage hasn't dropped
    - [x] Provide verification config / commands / resources
    - [x] Enable "Allow edits from maintainers" for this PR
    - [x] Update the messages below
    
    ***Is this ready for review?:*** YES
    ***Is it a breaking change?:*** NO

    Make processed input path absolute (#156)
    
    * Make processed input path absolute

commit 78c67ed835c1c3570b345597289a8e1c598797f2
Author: Van der Auwermeulen Grégoire <gregoirevandera@gmail.com>
Date:   Fri Jun 9 09:49:08 2017 +0200

    Add lifecycle hook for serverless offline start
    
    Serverless offline has 2 root commands to start :
    - `serverless offline` which triggers `offline:start` life cycle hook (This is working)
    - `serverless offline start` which triggers `offline:start:init` and  `offline:start:end` life cycle hooks (This is NOT working)
    
    The second one is important, because it has an event on start up and on end.
    If you want to work with serverless-offline, serverless-webpack and serverless-dynamodb-local. You need to call `sls offline start` which will also stop the db and stop serverless offline

commit 66662cef9a1779238cfee79e2e6a7e6bd69e4634
Author: Steven Yap <stevenyap@futureworkz.com>
Date:   Thu Nov 17 17:13:01 2016 +0700

    Server to cater to Lambda Proxy response
    
    If lambda proxy is enabled (which is by default in Serverless),
    the response returned in the lambda callback must be of the form:
    
    ```json
    {
      statusCode: 200,
      body: { /** data **/ }
    }
    ```
    
    The current server sends the entire response without separating
    the statusCode and body which is what this commit does.
    
    Ideally, we should detect if the lambda is using lambda proxy or not
    but I cannot find the flag to detect this setting.

    instead of event.query. This commit fixes the naming issue.
